  (function() {
    var isDOMContentLoaded = false;
    var DOMContentLoadedPromise = new Promise(function(resolve) {
      window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        isDOMContentLoaded = true;
        resolve();
      })
    });

    function wait(ms) {
      // if DOMContentLoaded already fired but wait function is called - we don't have to wait anymore (condition will not be met)
      if (!isDOMContentLoaded) {
        return Promise.race([
          new Promise(function (resolve) {
            setTimeout(resolve, ms)
          }),
          DOMContentLoadedPromise,
        ])
      } else {
        return Promise.resolve();
      }
    }

    var asyncFn = function(fn){
      var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
      var executor = function(resolve) {
        if (typeof window[fn] === 'undefined') {
          wait(1000).then(function() {executor(resolve)})
        } else {
          resolve(window[fn].apply(null, args.slice(1)))
        }
      };
      return new Promise(executor);
    }

    var asyncGet = function(prop){
      var executor = function(resolve) {
        if (typeof window[prop] === 'undefined') {
          return wait(1000).then(function() {executor(resolve)})
        } else {
          return resolve(window[prop])
        }
      };
      return new Promise(executor);
    };

    window.graphqlQuery = function(options, query) {
      var executor = function(resolve) {
        if (typeof window.GraphQl === 'undefined' || typeof  window.GraphQl.query !== 'function') {
          wait(1000).then(function() {executor(resolve)})
        } else {
          if (typeof query === 'string') {
            /* if we pass query is string - we are using queries from
               window.__GraphqlQueries, which should be defined and if it's
               undefined - we should wait */
            var tryExecuteQuery = function () {
              if (typeof window.__GraphqlQueries === 'undefined') {
                wait(1000).then(function () {
                  tryExecuteQuery(resolve)
                })
              } else {
                return resolve(window.GraphQl.query(Object.assign(options, {query: window.__GraphqlQueries[query]})))
              }
            }
            tryExecuteQuery(resolve);
          } else {
            return resolve(window.GraphQl.query(Object.assign(options, {query: query})))
          }
        }
      }
      return new Promise(executor);
    };

    window.storeDispatch = function(options) {
      var executor = function(resolve) {
        if (typeof window.__store === 'undefined' || typeof window.__store.dispatch !== 'function') {
          wait(1000).then(function() {executor(resolve)})
        } else {
          resolve(window.__store.dispatch(options))
        }
      };
      return new Promise(executor);
    };

    window.getLocalStorageItem = function(key) {
      var executor = function(resolve) {
        if (typeof window.localStorage === 'undefined' || typeof window.localStorage.getItem !== 'function') {
          wait(1000).then(function() {executor(resolve)})
        } else {
          resolve(window.localStorage.getItem(key))
        }
      }
      return new Promise(executor);
    }

    window.subscribeCurrencyFeed = function(options) {
      var executor = function(resolve) {
        if (typeof window.__currencyFeed === 'undefined') {
          wait(1000).then(function() {executor(resolve)})
        } else {
          resolve(window.__currencyFeed.subscribe(options))
        }
      };
      return new Promise(executor);
    };

    window.hydrateComponent = asyncFn.bind(null, "__hydrate_component_to_DOM_element");
    window.renderComponent = asyncFn.bind(null, "__render_component_to_DOM_element");
    window.getCurrentUser = asyncGet.bind(null, "__currentUser");
    window.getQueryParams = asyncGet.bind(null, "__queryParams");
    window.renderAdminComponent = asyncFn.bind(null, "__render_admin_component");
    window.getMarketplace = asyncGet.bind(null, "__marketplace");
    window.removeAdminComponent = asyncFn.bind(null, "__remove_admin_component");
    window.getCurrentCurrency = asyncGet.bind(null, "__currentCurrency");
  })()

			(function () {
				var splitTestsStorage = {

					get: function (component) {
						var splitTests = this._getAll();
						return splitTests[component];
					},

					set: function (component, data) {
						var splitTests = this._getAll();
						splitTests[component] = data;
						this._saveAll(splitTests);
					},

					remove: function (component) {
						var splitTests = this._getAll();
						delete splitTests[component];
						this._saveAll(splitTests);
					},

					_getAll: function () {
						this._createIfNotExists()
						return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('splitTests'));
					},

					_saveAll: function (data) {
						localStorage.setItem('splitTests', JSON.stringify(data));
					},

					_createIfNotExists: function () {
						if (!localStorage.getItem('splitTests')) {
							this._saveAll({});
						}
					}
				}

				function SplitTestVersionProvider() {
					var defaultValues = {
						TourSearchOnLandinPageAndCategoryPage: 'exists',
						CarsFunnel: 'new',
					};

					this.set = function (componentName, version, expirationDate) {
						if (expirationDate === undefined) {
							var msInADay = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
							expirationDate = new Date(Date.now() + msInADay);
						}
						if (expirationDate instanceof Date) {
							splitTestsStorage.set(componentName, {
								version: version,
								expirationUnixTimeMs: expirationDate.getTime()
							});
						}
						else {
							throw new Error('The expirationDate parameter should be instance of Date');
						}
					};

					this.get = function (componentName) {
						var experiment = splitTestsStorage.get(componentName);
						if (experiment) {
							if (experiment.expirationUnixTimeMs > Date.now()) {
								return experiment.version;
							} else {
								splitTestsStorage.remove(componentName);
							}
						}
						return defaultValues[componentName];
					};
				}
				window.__splitTestComponentVersion = new SplitTestVersionProvider();

				window.__onSplitTestsReady = function (cb, options) {
					if(options.isLocalStorageEnabled && localStorage.getItem(options.localStorageKey)) {
						cb();
					}

					if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
						return cb();
					}

					document.addEventListener('readystatechange', function () {
						if(document.readyState === 'complete') {
							return cb();
						}
					});
				}

			})()

Wait until page is ready functionality --><script data-whitelist="true">
/// $waitUntil
///      waits until a certain function returns true and then executes a code. checks the function periodically
/// parameters
///      check - a function that should return false or true
///      onComplete - a function to execute when the check function returns true
///      delay - time in milliseconds, specifies the time period between each check. default value is 100
///      timeout - time in milliseconds, specifies how long to wait and check the check function before giving up
function $waitUntil(check,onComplete,delay,timeout) {
  // if the check returns true, execute onComplete immediately
  if (check()) {
      onComplete();
      return;
  }

  if (!delay) delay=100;

  var timeoutPointer;
  var intervalPointer=setInterval(function () {
      if (!check()) return; // if check didn't return true, means we need another check in the next interval

      // if the check returned true, means we're done here. clear the interval and the timeout and execute onComplete
      clearInterval(intervalPointer);
      if (timeoutPointer) clearTimeout(timeoutPointer);
      onComplete();
  },delay);
  // if after timeout milliseconds function doesn't return true, abort
  if (timeout) timeoutPointer=setTimeout(function () {
      clearInterval(intervalPointer);
  },timeout);
}
</script><script data-whitelist="true">

}

I live inBorgarfjord west Iceland, where I work as a project leader at the cultural medieval center Snorrastofa in Reykholt. For th<span class="js-shave-char" style="float: none;"></span><span class="js-shave" style="display: none;">ose that don't know, Reykholt was the home of Snorri Sturluson, medieval writer and poet whom lived in Reykholt from 1206 to 1241. He was the author of the Edda, Heimskringla (History of the kings of Norway) and Egils Saga Skallagrimsson.
For me Snorri is the most amazing employer whom I proudly serve and constantly present in my every day life! He is absolutely still going strong at 835 years of age.
Please come and visit us at www.snorrastofa.is. We are open all weekdays during the winter and all days during summer. We have an exhibition about Snorri Sturluson and offer lectures for groups. I love to delve b<span class="js-shave-char" style="float: none;"></span><span class="js-shave" style="display: none;">elow the surface of things and to give people insight into Iceland's culture and its people. I have written about the Icelandic national character, the harsh lives of the Icelanders in the old days, the Icelandic language and how it reflects and is reflected in Icelandic culture, and Iceland's folk legends and how and where they originated. My latest book is called The Little Book of Tourists in Iceland, and it is chock-full of insights and tips to help all those who wish to tour Iceland safely, responsibly and in harmony with the locals. On this site I hope to share some tips and insights to help you gain a better understanding of the Icelanders, and the best practices for touring Iceland.</span></span></a><span><a class="abs-center click-me" href="/connect-with-locals/aldasigmunds">Read more</a></span></div></div></div><div class="col-xs-6 col-sm-4 col-md-3 col-lg-2 no-pad local" style="height: 257px;"><div class="lazyContainer"><noscript><img alt="Jorunn" class="img-responsive" height="237" src="https://guidetoiceland.imgix.net/264709/x/0/11295620-10153238941081702-3550596219743129921-n-jpg-oh-a5df808ba89507cb33f99b00c1a608a6oe-568cf0bc-gda-1452655058-9873a5b474c5bbbb3d86cda4e7b2a9b0-jpg?auto=compress%2Cformat&amp;ch=Width%2CDPR&amp;crop=faces&amp;dpr=1&amp;fit=crop&amp;h=300&amp;ixlib=php-3.0.0&amp;w=300&amp;s=0f648f3158e943a8193e6373907996ba" width="313"/></noscript><img alt="Jorunn" class="lazyload img-responsive" data-src="https://guidetoiceland.imgix.net/264709/x/0/11295620-10153238941081702-3550596219743129921-n-jpg-oh-a5df808ba89507cb33f99b00c1a608a6oe-568cf0bc-gda-1452655058-9873a5b474c5bbbb3d86cda4e7b2a9b0-jpg?auto=compress%2Cformat&amp;ch=Width%2CDPR&amp;crop=faces&amp;dpr=1&amp;fit=crop&amp;h=300&amp;ixlib=php-3.0.0&amp;w=300&amp;s=0f648f3158e943a8193e6373907996ba" height="237" src="" width="313"/></div><span><a class="abs-center click-me" href="/connect-with-locals/jorunnsg">Jorunn</a></span><div class="mask"><div class="more-info"><a class="local" href="/connect-with-locals/jorunnsg" style="height: 257px;"><span class="excerpt" style="">My name is Jorunn and I live in Reykjavik. 			if (i === 'length' || !tours.hasOwnProperty(i)) {

			tourElement = tours[i];

			var tourId = tourElement.getAttribute('data-tour_id');

					id: parseInt(tourId),

	(function(window, undefined) {
		var api = 'youtube';
		var uri = 'NN2yWrSFZlg';

		var cfg = {
			enable: true,
			api: (api && api.length) ? api : null,
			uri: (uri && uri.length) ? uri : null,
			isMobile: false		};

		cfg.enable = (cfg.enable && cfg.api && cfg.uri && !cfg.isMobile);

		window.videoConfig = cfg;

		function resize_pictures_section() {
			var width = window.innerWidth;

			if(width < 756) {
				$('#pictures-section .pictures').height('200px');
			}
			else if(width < 980) {
				$('#pictures-section .pictures').height('300px');
			}
			else {
				$('#pictures-section .pictures').height('400px');
			}
		}

		if(videoConfig.enable) {
			function showFrontActions() {
				if(videoConfig.api === 'vimeo') {
					$('#video_wrapper').animate({
						opacity: 0,
						visibility: 'hidden'
					}, 400);
				} else {
					$('#video_wrapper').fadeOut(400);
				}
			}

			function hideFrontActions() {
				if(videoConfig.api === 'vimeo') {
					$('#video_wrapper').animate({
						opacity: 1,
						visibility: 'visible'
					}, 400);
				} else {
					$('#video_wrapper').fadeIn(400);
				}
			}

			function resizeVideo() {
				var docWidth = $('#banner-image').width();
				// var newWidth = docWidth * 1.2;
				var newWidth = docWidth;
				var newMargin = (newWidth - docWidth) / 2;
				$('#video_wrapper').css({
					width: newWidth,
					marginLeft: newMargin * -1
				}).attr('width', newWidth);

				var ratio = 510 / 854;
				var docHeight = $('#banner-image').height();
				// var newHeight = docHeight * 1.2;
				var newHeight = (newWidth * ratio);
				var newMarginTop = (newHeight -docHeight ) / 2;

				if(videoConfig.api === 'youtube') {
					$('#video_wrapper').css({
						height: newHeight,
						marginTop: newMarginTop * -1
					}).attr('height', newHeight);
				}
				else if(videoConfig.api === 'vimeo') {
					$('#video_wrapper').css({
						height: newHeight,
						margin: '0 auto',
						marginTop: newMarginTop * -1,
						overflow: 'hidden'
					}).attr('height', newHeight);

					// $("#vimeo_player").attr('height', newHeight+200).attr('width', newWidth).css({ display:'block', margin:'0 auto', marginTop:'-100px' });

					$("#video_wrapper")
						.find("#vimeo_player")
						.attr('height', newHeight + 200)
						.attr('width', newWidth)
						.css({
							display: 'block',
							margin:'0 auto',
							marginTop:'-100px'
						});
				}
			}

			function resize_video_container() {
				var ratio = 510 / 854;
				var container = $("#banner-image:not(.banner-search-widget)");
				var width = container.width();
				container.height(width * ratio);

				if(width < 756) {
					container.height('200px');
				}
				else if(width < 980) {
					container.height('350px');
				}
				else {
					container.height('600px');
				}
			}

			$(window).resize(function(){
				resize_video_container();
				resize_pictures_section();
				resizeVideo();
			}).resize();

			if(videoConfig.api === 'vimeo') {
				$(document).ready(function() {
					$.getScript('https://f.vimeocdn.com/js/froogaloop2.min.js', function() {
						var player, playerOrigin;

						var iframe_element = document.createElement('iframe');

						iframe_element.setAttribute('id', 'vimeo_player')
						iframe_element.setAttribute('src', 'https://player.vimeo.com/video/' + videoConfig.uri + '?autoplay=0&badge=0&byline=0&portrait=0&title=0')
						iframe_element.setAttribute('frameborder', '0');
						iframe_element.setAttribute('webkitallowfullscreen', 'webkitallowfullscreen');
						iframe_element.setAttribute('mozallowfullscreen', 'mozallowfullscreen');
						iframe_element.setAttribute('allowfullscreen', 'allowfullscreen');
						iframe_element.setAttribute('height','100%');
						$("#video_wrapper").append(iframe_element);

						player = $("#vimeo_player");
						playerOrigin = '*';

						if(window.addEventListener) {
							window.addEventListener('message', onMessageReceived, false);
						} else {
							window.attachEvent('onmessage', onMessageReceived, false);
						}

						// Handle messages received from the player
						function onMessageReceived(event) {
							// Handle messages from the vimeo player only
							if(!(/^https?:\/\/player.vimeo.com/).test(event.origin)) {
								return false;
							}

							if(playerOrigin === '*') {
								playerOrigin = event.origin;
							}

							if(typeof event.data === 'string') {
								var data = JSON.parse(event.data);
							} else {
								var data = event.data;
							}

							switch (data.event) {
								case 'ready':
									onReady();
									break;
								case 'ended':
								case 'finish':
									showFrontActions();
									$('.button-group .play').show(400);
									$('.button-group .mute').hide(400);
									$('.button-group .unmute').hide(400);
									$('.button-group .skip').hide(400);
									break;
							}
						}

						// Helper function for sending a message to the player
						function postPlayer(action, value) {
							var data = {
								method: action
							};

							if(value || value === 0) {
								data.value = value;
							}

							var message = JSON.stringify(data);
							player[0].contentWindow.postMessage(data, playerOrigin);
						}

						function onReady() {
							postPlayer('setVolume', 0);
							postPlayer('play', null);
							postPlayer('addEventListener', 'finish');
							resize_video_container();
							resize_pictures_section();
							resizeVideo();
						}

						function onFinish() {
							setTimeout(function() {
								postPlayer('seekTo', 0);
							}, 800);
						}

						$('.button-group .skip').click(function(){
							$(this).hide(400);
							$('.play').show(400);
							$('.button-group .mute').hide(400);
							$('.button-group .unmute').hide(400);
							postPlayer('pause');
							setTimeout(function() {
								postPlayer('seekTo', 0.0001);
							}, 800);
							showFrontActions();
							$(this).fadeOut(400);
						});

						$('.button-group .play').click(function() {
							$(this).hide(400);
							$('.skip').show(400);
							postPlayer('play');
							postPlayer('setVolume', 1.0);
							$('.button-group .mute').show(400);
							hideFrontActions();
							$(this).fadeOut(400);
						});

						$('.button-group .unmute').click(function() {
							$(this).hide(400, function() {
								$('.button-group .mute').show(400)
							});
							postPlayer('setVolume', 1.0);
						});

						$('.button-group .mute').click(function() {
							$(this).hide(400, function() {
								$('.button-group .unmute').show(400)
							});
							postPlayer('setVolume', 0);
						});
					});
				});
			}
			else if(videoConfig.api === 'youtube') {
				var tag = document.createElement('script');
				tag.src = "https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api";
				var firstScriptTag = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
				firstScriptTag.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, firstScriptTag);
				var video;

				function onYouTubeIframeAPIReady() {
					video = new YT.Player('video_wrapper', {
						playerVars: {
							'autoplay': 0,
							'controls': 0,
							'disablekb': 1,
							'autohide': 1,
							'wmode': 'transparent',
							'modestbranding': 1,
							'showinfo': 0,
							'rel': 0,
							'enablejsapi': 1,
							'allowfullscreen': false,
							'iv_load_policy': 3,
							'html5': 1,
							'loop': 0,
							'fs': 0
						},
						videoId: videoConfig.uri || '-SJIOfzbQbQ',
						events: {
							'onReady': onPlayerReady,
							'onStateChange': onPlayerStateChange
						}
					});
				}

				function onPlayerReady(event) {
					event.target.mute();
					event.target.playVideo();
				}

				function onPlayerStateChange(event) {
					if(event.data === 0) {
						showFrontActions();
						$('.button-group .play').show(400);
						$('.button-group .mute').hide(400);
						$('.button-group .unmute').hide(400);
						$('.button-group .skip').hide(400);
					}

					if(event.data === 2) {
						showFrontActions();
						$('.button-group .play').show(400);
						$('.button-group .mute').hide(400);
						$('.button-group .unmute').hide(400);
						$('.button-group .skip').hide(400);
					}
				}

				$('.button-group .skip').click(function() {
					$(this).hide(400);
					$('.play').show(400);
					$('.button-group .mute').hide(400);
					$('.button-group .unmute').hide(400);
					video.stopVideo();
					showFrontActions();
					$(this).fadeOut(400);
				});

				$('.button-group .play').click(function() {
					$(this).hide(400);
					$('.skip').show(400);
					video.playVideo();
					video.unMute();
					$('.button-group .mute').show(400);
					hideFrontActions();
					$(this).fadeOut(400);
				});

				$('.button-group .unmute').click(function() {
					video.unMute();
					$(this).hide();
					$('.button-group .mute').show();
				});

				$('.button-group .mute').click(function() {
					video.mute();
					$(this).hide();
					$('.button-group .unmute').show();
				});
			}
		} else {
			$(document).ready(function() {
				$(window).resize(function() {
					var container = $("#banner-image:not(.banner-search-widget)");
					var width = container.width();

					if(width < 756) {
						container.height('200px');
					}
					else if(width < 980) {
						container.height('350px');
					}
					else {
						container.height('600px');
					}

					resize_pictures_section();
				}).resize();
			});
		}

	var closeImageGallery = function(){
		var ImageGalleryWrapper = document.getElementById('react-image-gallery-wrapper');
		if(ImageGalleryWrapper) {
			window.renderComponent(ImageGalleryWrapper, 'ImageGalleryWrapper', {
				images: [],
				isOpen: false,
			})
		}
	};

	var onAfterOpen = function(clickedPhoto){
		clickedPhoto.focus();
	};

	var showImageGallery = function(clickedPhoto, imageContainer) {
		const clickedSrc = clickedPhoto.attr("react-gallery-href");
		var photoIndex = 0;
		var imageGalleryItems = [];

		$(imageContainer).each(function (index, value) {
			var item = {};
			item.url = $(value).attr("react-gallery-href");
			item.description = $(value).attr("title") || $(value).find("img").attr('title');

			imageGalleryItems.push(item);

			if(item.url === clickedSrc) {
				photoIndex = index;
			}
		});

		var ImageGalleryWrapper = document.getElementById('react-image-gallery-wrapper');
		if(ImageGalleryWrapper) {
			window.renderComponent(ImageGalleryWrapper, 'ImageGalleryWrapper', {
				images: imageGalleryItems,
				photoIndex: photoIndex,
				isOpen: true,
				onAfterOpen: onAfterOpen(clickedPhoto),
				onClose: closeImageGallery,
			})
		}
	};
